[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory access resulting in a segmentation fault.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important observations  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The input blob contains repeated “%x”, “%n”, and “%s” sequences followed by [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpadding [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`A…A`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and TLV-like headers, suggesting user-supplied data is reaching a [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m, ENC_BIG_ENDIAN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m698[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39moffset += [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m699[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m700[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mbat_vis_tree, hf_bat_max_tq_v23, tvb, offset, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m, ENC_BIG_ENDIAN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m701[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m*offset += [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;*[0m[35m/[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m702[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m703[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m704[0m[39m:    [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mvis_packeth_raw_data_size > [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvis_packeth_raw_data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m > [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m705[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[1;35mfprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstderr, d_output_buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Both `dissect_bat_vis_v23` and `dissect_bat_vis_v24` build a human-readable [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmessage in `d_output_buffer` that embeds untrusted packet bytes in [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`vis_packeth_raw_data`. They then invoke[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```c[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mfprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstderr, d_output_buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       ```[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     using `d_output_buffer` as the format string. Any “%” in packet data is [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minterpreted by `fprintf`, causing “wild-addr-read” crashes under AddressSanitizer.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This is a classic format-string vulnerability: untrusted input is used [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdirectly as a format specifier list.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preservation of Functionality[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We still want to log the same message [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfor debugging[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m into `stderr`, including[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe raw data, but we must prevent format-string interpretation.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must not alter the harness or fuzzing logic, nor drop any legitimate [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality of the dissector; only the debug/log print calls are modified.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Steps[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Ensure Null-Termination of Raw Data[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Immediately after copying `vis_packeth_raw_data_size` bytes into [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`vis_packeth_raw_data`, explicitly null-terminate the buffer:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```c[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* After the loop that does vis_packeth_raw_data[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = …; *[0m[35m/[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvis_packeth_raw_data_size >= [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvis_packeth_raw_data[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            vis_packeth_raw_data[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvis_packeth_raw_data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            vis_packeth_raw_data[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mvis_packeth_raw_data_size[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This prevents any over-reads if the packet fills the buffer exactly.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Change Uncontrolled Format Call to Controlled Call[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - In both `dissect_bat_vis_v23` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line ~[0m[1;36m705[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `dissect_bat_vis_v24` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39maround line ~[0m[1;36m705[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, replace:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```c[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mvis_packeth_raw_data_size > [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvis_packeth_raw_data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m > [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mfprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstderr, d_output_buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        with:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```c[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mvis_packeth_raw_data_size > [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvis_packeth_raw_data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m > [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mfprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mstderr, [0m[32m"%s"[0m[39m, d_output_buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - By supplying `[0m[32m"%s"[0m[39m` as the format, `d_output_buffer` is treated as plain [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdata and not re-parsed for format specifiers.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Using a fixed format string [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[32m"%s"[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ensures that any “%” characters embedded [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min `d_output_buffer` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwhich itself embeds raw packet data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are not interpreted by [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`fprintf`. This directly addresses the AddressSanitizer “wild-addr-read” by [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39meliminating format-string parsing on attacker-controlled input.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Explicitly null-terminating `vis_packeth_raw_data` also prevents potential [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mover-reads when `%s` is processed by `snprintf`.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The logic that decides when to log [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`raw_data_size > [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m && [0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m > [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremains unchanged; only the printing mechanism is hardened.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All other dissector behavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39mTLV parsing, tree construction, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntouched.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side-Effects and Mitigations[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The debug output remains identical in content and condition; only its safety [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis improved.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - There is negligible performance impact: one extra null-termination branch and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafe `fprintf` call.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No existing tests or harness logic will be broken.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References in Codebase[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Similar pattern in v23 and v24: both versions read raw data into a fixed [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer, build `d_output_buffer` via `snprintf`, then `fprintf`. This patch aligns [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe two to a safe, consistent practice.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                   [0m[2;36m [0m[34mINFO    [0m Prism Supervisor Routing: TeamStatus.EVALUATE -> TeamStatus.END                      ]8;id=782;file:///home/qqor/crete/packages/crete/framework/agent/services/prism/__init__.py\[2m__init__.py[0m]8;;\[2m:[0m]8;id=70824;file:///home/qqor/crete/packages/crete/framework/agent/services/prism/__init__.py#160\[2m160[0m]8;;\
